table.MsoNormalTable\r\n	{mso-style-name:普通表格;\r\n	mso-tstyle-rowband-size:0;\r\n	mso-tstyle-colband-size:0;\r\n	mso-style-noshow:yes;\r\n	mso-style-priority:99;\r\n	mso-style-parent:\"\";\r\n	mso-padding-alt:0cm 5.4pt 0cm 5.4pt;\r\n	mso-para-margin:0cm;\r\n	mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;\r\n	mso-pagination:widow-orphan;\r\n	font-size:10.5pt;\r\n	font-family:宋体;\r\n	letter-spacing:-.25pt;}\r\n</style>\r\n<![endif]-->\r\n<p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-indent:23.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:2.0;\r\nline-height:150%\">\r\n	<span style=\"font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.5pt;\r\nline-height:150%\">近几年来，由真菌（主要是念珠菌、隐球菌、曲霉菌和孢子菌等）感染引发的疾病越来越引起人们的重视。据统计，目前全球有近<span lang=\"EN-US\">3</span>亿人患有不同程度真菌引起的相关疾病，全球每年因真菌感染及其并发症导致的死亡人数或超过<span lang=\"EN-US\">160</span>万，与结核病导致的死亡人数相近。而英国政府资助的一项研究表明，如果不制定政策来减缓包括真菌等引起的耐药性的上升，到<span lang=\"EN-US\">2050</span>年，全球将有<span lang=\"EN-US\">1000</span>万人死于耐药性，超过预计将因癌症死亡的<span lang=\"EN-US\">800</span>万人。因此，真菌对目前已知的抗菌药物耐药性的增加，是当今社会要面临的一项重大问题；而像耳念珠菌这样具有多重耐药性念珠菌&mdash;&mdash;超级细菌的出现，更是全球健康要面对的一项严重挑战。<span lang=\"EN-US\"><span style=\"mso-spacerun:yes\">&nbsp;&nbsp; </span></span></span></p>\r\n<p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-indent:23.1pt;mso-char-indent-count:2.0;\r\nline-height:150%\">\r\n	<b style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight:normal\"><span lang=\"EN-US\" style=\"font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.5pt;line-height:150%\">&nbsp;</span></b></p>\r\n<p align=\"left\" class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align:left\">\r\n	<b style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight:\r\nnormal\"><span style=\"font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.5pt;font-family:\r\n&quot;微软雅黑&quot;,sans-serif;color:red\">流行病学特征： </span></b><b style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight:\r\nnormal\"><span lang=\"EN-US\" style=\"font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.5pt;\r\nfont-family:&quot;微软雅黑&quot;,sans-serif\"><span style=\"mso-spacerun:yes\">&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></b><span lang=\"EN-US\" style=\"font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.5pt;font-family:&quot;微软雅黑&quot;,sans-serif\"><span style=\"mso-spacerun:yes\">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span style=\"mso-spacerun:yes\">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></p>\r\n<p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height:150%\">\r\n	<span lang=\"EN-US\" style=\"font-size:\r\n12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.5pt;line-height:150%\"><span style=\"mso-spacerun:yes\">&nbsp; </span><span style=\"mso-spacerun:yes\">&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span><span style=\"font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.5pt;line-height:150%\">目前，已知不少于<span lang=\"EN-US\">9</span>种常见的念珠菌能引起人或动物的感染<span lang=\"EN-US\">,</span>均为条件致病菌。它们是白色念珠菌、热带念珠菌、克柔念珠菌、星形念珠菌、高里念珠菌、光滑念珠菌、近平滑念珠菌、乳酒念珠菌和耳念珠菌等。其中引起人类念珠菌病的主要是白色念珠菌，而耐药性最强的是耳念珠菌。近年来由于不合理使用抗生素、肿瘤化疗、艾滋病的流行和器官移植等使念珠菌的感染机会逐年上升，念珠菌主要引起真菌败血症、泌尿系统感染和全身感染等严重疾病，在医院血液感染中列第四位，病死率列第一位，可达<span lang=\"EN-US\">40%</span>以上，在<span lang=\"EN-US\">ICU</span>中最常发生。目前，临床光滑念珠菌和耳念珠菌检出率也有明显上升趋势。</span></p>\r\n<span style=\"font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.5pt;font-family:宋体;\r\nmso-bidi-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:\r\nZH-CN;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA\">下面给出的是一项结合国内外典型研究的统计表，从中大致可以了解常见念珠菌的分型以及其耐药性。</span><br />\r\n<p align=\"center\" class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align:center;line-height:150%\">\r\n	<span style=\"font-size:14px;\"><b><span style=\"font-family:&quot;微软雅黑&quot;,sans-serif;color:black;background:white\">一项念珠菌的分类占比及其耐药性的统计分析</span></b></span></p>\r\n<div style=\"text-align: center;\">\r\n	<span style=\"text-indent:23.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:2.0;\r\nline-height:150%\">\r\n		<span style=\"font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.5pt;\r\nline-height:150%\">超级病菌&mdash;&mdash;耳念珠菌是一种新出现的、多重耐药的病原体，近年来在世界范围内造成多起感染暴发，它通常发生在重症监护病房<span lang=\"EN-US\">(</span></span><span lang=\"EN-US\" style=\"font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:\r\n10.5pt;line-height:150%;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif\">Intensive Care Unit</span><span style=\"font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.5pt;line-height:\r\n150%\">，缩写为</span><span lang=\"EN-US\" style=\"font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:\r\n10.5pt;line-height:150%;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif\">ICU</span><span lang=\"EN-US\" style=\"font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.5pt;line-height:150%\">)</span><span style=\"font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.5pt;line-height:150%\">。<span lang=\"EN-US\">2009</span>年在一位日本患者的耳道中首次检出，并于<span lang=\"EN-US\">2011</span>年在韩国造成<span lang=\"EN-US\">3</span>例血流感染。<span lang=\"EN-US\">2012</span>年<span lang=\"EN-US\">3</span>月<span lang=\"EN-US\">-2013</span>年<span lang=\"EN-US\">7</span>月，耳念菌首次在委内瑞拉爆发，涉及<span lang=\"EN-US\">18</span>名患者；此后全球爆发了多起耳念菌感染事件。 全基因组测序揭示了不同大陆和次大陆上真菌的遗传分离，其中包括东亚、南亚、南美和南非。自<span lang=\"EN-US\">2004</span>年以来，国际上共收集<span lang=\"EN-US\">15,271</span>种侵入性耳念珠菌的亚型，研究者从中重新鉴定了<span lang=\"EN-US\">4</span>种亚型，最终认定耳念珠菌业已成为新的严重临床问题。</span></p>\r\n	<p class=\"MsoNormal\">\r\n		<span lang=\"EN-US\" style=\"font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:\r\n10.5pt\">&nbsp;</span></p>\r\n	<p align=\"left\" class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align:left\">\r\n		<b style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight:\r\nnormal\"><span style=\"font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.5pt;font-family:\r\n&quot;微软雅黑&quot;,sans-serif;color:red\">主要危险人群、危险因素及危害证据：</span></b></p>\r\n	<p align=\"left\" class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align:left\">\r\n		<b style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight:\r\nnormal\"><span lang=\"EN-US\" style=\"font-size:5.5pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.5pt;\r\nfont-family:&quot;微软雅黑&quot;,sans-serif;color:red\">&nbsp;</span></b></p>\r\n	<p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height:150%\">\r\n		<b><span lang=\"EN-US\" style=\"font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%;color:red;background:white\">1.</span></b><b><span lang=\"EN-US\" style=\"font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%;font-family:Wingdings;\r\nmso-fareast-font-family:Wingdings;mso-bidi-font-family:Wingdings;color:black;\r\nletter-spacing:0pt\"><span lfo1;background:white\">\r\n		<span style=\"font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%;\r\nmso-bidi-font-family:宋体;color:black;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-bidi-font-weight:\r\nbold\"><span lang=\"EN-US\" style=\"font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.5pt;line-height:150%;\r\nfont-family:Wingdings;mso-fareast-font-family:Wingdings;mso-bidi-font-family:\r\nWingdings;color:black;letter-spacing:0pt\"><span class=\"MsoListParagraph\" style=\"margin-left:21.0pt;text-align:left;\r\ntext-indent:-21.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:0;line-height:150%;mso-pagination:\r\nwidow-orphan;mso-list:l0 level1 lfo2;background:white\">\r\n		<span lang=\"EN-US\" style=\"font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.5pt;line-height:150%;\r\nfont-family:Wingdings;mso-fareast-font-family:Wingdings;mso-bidi-font-family:\r\nWingdings;color:black;letter-spacing:0pt\"><span style=\"mso-list:Ignore\">&lt;&gt;</span></span><span lang=\"EN-US\" style=\"font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.5pt;line-height:150%;\r\nmso-bidi-font-family:宋体;color:black;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-bidi-font-weight:\r\nbold\">ICU</span><span style=\"font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.5pt;\r\nline-height:150%;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;color:black;letter-spacing:0pt;\r\nmso-bidi-font-weight:bold\">停留；</span></p>\r\n	<p align=\"left\" class=\"MsoListParagraph\" style=\"margin-left:21.0pt;text-align:left;\r\ntext-indent:-21.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:0;line-height:150%;mso-pagination:\r\nwidow-orphan;mso-list:l0 level1 lfo2;background:white\">\r\n		<span lang=\"EN-US\" style=\"font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%;font-family:Wingdings;\r\nmso-fareast-font-family:Wingdings;mso-bidi-font-family:Wingdings;color:black;\r\nletter-spacing:0pt\"><span style=\"mso-list:Ignore\">&lt;&gt;</span></span><span lang=\"EN-US\" style=\"font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%;font-family:Wingdings;\r\nmso-fareast-font-family:Wingdings;mso-bidi-font-family:Wingdings;color:black;\r\nletter-spacing:0pt;mso-bidi-font-weight:bold\"><span style=\"mso-list:Ignore\"><span style=\"font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;\">&nbsp;</span></span></span><span lang=\"EN-US\" style=\"font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.5pt;line-height:150%;\r\nfont-family:Wingdings;mso-fareast-font-family:Wingdings;mso-bidi-font-family:\r\nWingdings;color:black;letter-spacing:0pt\"><span style=\"mso-list:Ignore\"><span style=\"font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;\"> </span></span></span><span style=\"font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.5pt;line-height:150%;mso-bidi-font-family:\r\n宋体;color:black;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-bidi-font-weight:bold\">使用中心静脉导管；</span></p>\r\n	<p align=\"left\" class=\"MsoListParagraph\" style=\"margin-left:21.0pt;text-align:left;\r\ntext-indent:-21.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:0;line-height:150%;mso-pagination:\r\nwidow-orphan;mso-list:l0 level1 lfo2;background:white\">\r\n		<span lang=\"EN-US\" style=\"font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.5pt;line-height:150%;\r\nfont-family:Wingdings;mso-fareast-font-family:Wingdings;mso-bidi-font-family:\r\nWingdings;color:black;letter-spacing:0pt\"><span style=\"mso-list:Ignore\">&lt;&gt;<span style=\"font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;\"> </span></span></span><span style=\"font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.5pt;line-height:150%;mso-bidi-font-family:\r\n宋体;color:black;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-bidi-font-weight:bold\">免疫抑制治疗；</span></p>\r\n	<p align=\"left\" class=\"MsoListParagraph\" style=\"margin-left:21.0pt;text-align:left;\r\ntext-indent:-21.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:0;line-height:150%;mso-pagination:\r\nwidow-orphan;mso-list:l0 level1 lfo2;background:white\">\r\n		<span lang=\"EN-US\" style=\"font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.5pt;line-height:150%;\r\nfont-family:Wingdings;mso-fareast-font-family:Wingdings;mso-bidi-font-family:\r\nWingdings;color:black;letter-spacing:0pt\"><span style=\"mso-list:Ignore\">&lt;&gt;<span style=\"font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;\"> </span></span></span><span style=\"font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.5pt;line-height:150%;mso-bidi-font-family:\r\n宋体;color:black;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-bidi-font-weight:bold\">使用导尿管；</span></p>\r\n	<p align=\"left\" class=\"MsoListParagraph\" style=\"margin-left:21.0pt;text-align:left;\r\ntext-indent:-21.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:0;line-height:150%;mso-pagination:\r\nwidow-orphan;mso-list:l0 level1 lfo2;background:white\">\r\n		<span lang=\"EN-US\" style=\"font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%;font-family:Wingdings;\r\nmso-fareast-font-family:Wingdings;mso-bidi-font-family:Wingdings;color:black;\r\nletter-spacing:0pt\"><span style=\"mso-list:Ignore\">&lt;&gt;</span></span><span lang=\"EN-US\" style=\"font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%;font-family:Wingdings;\r\nmso-fareast-font-family:Wingdings;mso-bidi-font-family:Wingdings;color:black;\r\nletter-spacing:0pt;mso-bidi-font-weight:bold\"><span style=\"mso-list:Ignore\"><span style=\"font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;\">&nbsp;</span></span></span><span lang=\"EN-US\" style=\"font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.5pt;line-height:150%;\r\nfont-family:Wingdings;mso-fareast-font-family:Wingdings;mso-bidi-font-family:\r\nWingdings;color:black;letter-spacing:0pt\"><span style=\"mso-list:Ignore\"><span style=\"font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;\">&nbsp; </span></span></span><span style=\"font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.5pt;line-height:150%;mso-bidi-font-family:\r\n宋体;color:black;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-bidi-font-weight:bold\">近期手术。</span></p>\r\n	<p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height:150%\">\r\n		<span lang=\"EN-US\" style=\"font-size:\r\n12.0pt;line-height:150%\">&nbsp;</span></p>\r\n	<p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height:150%\">\r\n		<b><span lang=\"EN-US\" style=\"font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%;color:red;background:white\">3.</span></b><b><span style=\"font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%;color:red;background:white\">主要危害证据：</span></b></p>\r\n	<p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:2.0;\r\nline-height:150%;mso-pagination:widow-orphan;background:white\">\r\n		<span style=\"font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;color:black;\r\nletter-spacing:0pt;mso-bidi-font-weight:bold\">在我国，目前已经报告的耳念珠菌患者有<span lang=\"EN-US\">18</span>人，其中北京<span lang=\"EN-US\">3</span>人，沈阳<span lang=\"EN-US\">15</span>人，南方地区暂未发现确诊病例。</span></p>\r\n	<p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-indent:23.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:2.0;\r\nline-height:150%\">\r\n		<span style=\"font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.5pt;\r\nline-height:150%\">在美国，根据美国疾控中心<span lang=\"EN-US\">CDC</span>的数据，截止到<span lang=\"EN-US\">2019</span>年<span lang=\"EN-US\">2</span>月底，全美耳念珠菌确诊病例有<span lang=\"EN-US\">587</span>例，其中纽约州有<span lang=\"EN-US\">309</span>例，占<span lang=\"EN-US\">53%</span>，新泽西州有<span lang=\"EN-US\">104</span>例。</span></p>\r\n	<p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-indent:23.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:2.0;\r\nline-height:150%\">\r\n		<span style=\"font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.5pt;\r\nline-height:150%\">据英国《泰晤士报》报道，在芝加哥的一些养老院中，一半住户的耳念珠菌检测结果为阳性。</span></p>\r\n	<p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-indent:23.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:2.0;\r\nline-height:150%\">\r\n		<span style=\"font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.5pt;\r\nline-height:150%\">在欧洲，耳念珠菌曾在英国、西班牙、挪威和德国检出。<span lang=\"EN-US\">2013</span>年到<span lang=\"EN-US\">2017</span>年，欧洲疾病控制和预防中心（<span lang=\"EN-US\">ECDC</span>）报告了来自几个国家的<span lang=\"EN-US\">620</span>个欧洲耳念珠菌病例。</span></p>\r\n	<p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height:150%\">\r\n		<span style=\"font-size:12.0pt;\r\nmso-bidi-font-size:10.5pt;line-height:150%\">最大的一次感染暴发发生于<span lang=\"EN-US\">2015</span>年<span lang=\"EN-US\">4</span>月至<span lang=\"EN-US\">2016</span>年<span lang=\"EN-US\">11</span>月期间，地点在伦敦的一家心胸外科<span lang=\"EN-US\">ICU</span>，涉及<span lang=\"EN-US\">72</span>位患者。</span></p>\r\n	<p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-indent:23.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:2.0;\r\nline-height:150%\">\r\n		<span lang=\"EN-US\" style=\"font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:\r\n10.5pt;line-height:150%\">2016</span><span style=\"font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:\r\n10.5pt;line-height:150%\">年<span lang=\"EN-US\">6</span>月英国曾发出警报，牛津大学附属医院<span lang=\"EN-US\">NHS</span>信托基金组织的一项回顾性调查中发现在<span lang=\"EN-US\">2015</span>年<span lang=\"EN-US\">2</span>月<span lang=\"EN-US\">2</span>日至<span lang=\"EN-US\">2016</span>年<span lang=\"EN-US\">10</span>月<span lang=\"EN-US\">16</span>日期间，有<span lang=\"EN-US\">4</span>位耳念珠菌定植患者和<span lang=\"EN-US\">5</span>位感染患者。这<span lang=\"EN-US\">9</span>位患者中，<span lang=\"EN-US\">8</span>位在诊断前曾入住神经科<span lang=\"EN-US\">ICU</span>。</span></p>\r\n	<p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-indent:23.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:2.0;\r\nline-height:150%\">\r\n		<span style=\"font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.5pt;\r\nline-height:150%\">由于目前新型抗真菌的药物研发尚无令人鼓舞的进展，所以一般患者的死亡率可达<span lang=\"EN-US\">50%</span>，脑脊液感染患者的死亡率可能高达<span lang=\"EN-US\">72%</span>。</span></p>\r\n	<p class=\"MsoNormal\">\r\n		<span lang=\"EN-US\" style=\"font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:\r\n10.5pt\">&nbsp;</span></p>\r\n	<p align=\"left\" class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align:left;line-height:200%\">\r\n		<b style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight:normal\"><span style=\"font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:\r\n10.5pt;line-height:200%;font-family:&quot;微软雅黑&quot;,sans-serif;color:red\">权威观点：</span></b></p>\r\n	<p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-indent:23.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:2.0;\r\nline-height:150%\">\r\n		<span style=\"font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%;color:#333333;\r\nbackground:white;mso-bidi-font-weight:bold\">美国<span lang=\"EN-US\">CDC</span>认为，耳念珠菌会给全球健康都带来严重威胁。基于以下三点要密切关注这一真菌：</span></p>\r\n	<p align=\"left\" class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align:left;line-height:150%\">\r\n		<span lang=\"EN-US\" style=\"font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%;color:#333333;background:\r\nwhite\">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 1.</span><span style=\"font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%;\r\ncolor:#333333;background:white\">具有多重抗药性。耳念珠菌对一些常用于念珠菌感染的抗真菌药有抗药性。</span><br />\r\n		&nbsp;</p>\r\n	<p align=\"left\" class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align:left;line-height:150%\">\r\n		<span style=\"font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%;\r\ncolor:#333333;background:white\"><!--[if gte mso 9]><xml>\r\n <o:OfficeDocumentSettings>\r\n <w:LsdException Locked=\"false\" SemiHidden=\"true\" UnhideWhenUsed=\"true\"\r\n   Name=\"Unresolved Mention\"/>\r\n  <w:LsdException Locked=\"false\" SemiHidden=\"true\" UnhideWhenUsed=\"true\"\r\n   Name=\"Smart Link\"/>\r\n </w:LatentStyles>\r\n</xml><![endif]--><!--[if gte mso 10]>\r\n<style>\r\n /* Style Definitions */\r\n table.MsoNormalTable\r\n	{mso-style-name:普通表格;\r\n	mso-tstyle-rowband-size:0;\r\n	mso-tstyle-colband-size:0;\r\n	mso-style-noshow:yes;\r\n	mso-style-priority:99;\r\n	mso-style-parent:\"\";\r\n	mso-padding-alt:0cm 5.4pt 0cm 5.4pt;\r\n	mso-para-margin:0cm;\r\n	mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;\r\n	mso-pagination:widow-orphan;\r\n	font-size:10.5pt;\r\n	font-family:宋体;\r\n	letter-spacing:-.25pt;}\r\n</style>\r\n<![endif]--></span></p>\r\n	<p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-left:11.55pt;text-indent:-11.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:\r\n-1.0;line-height:150%\">\r\n		<span style=\"font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%;\r\ncolor:#333333;background:white\"><span lang=\"EN-US\" style=\"font-size:12.0pt;line-height:\r\n150%;color:#333333;background:white\">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; &nbsp; 2. </span><span style=\"font-size:\r\n12.0pt;line-height:150%;color:#333333;background:white\">难以通过标准实验方法鉴定。只有通过实验室的特殊技术才能鉴别耳念珠菌，而错误的鉴别结果则会导致错误的治疗方法。</span></span></p>\r\n	<p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-left:11.55pt;text-indent:-11.55pt;mso-char-indent-count:\r\n-1.0;line-height:150%\">\r\n		<span style=\"font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%;\r\ncolor:#333333;background:white\"><span lang=\"EN-US\" style=\"font-size:12.0pt;line-height:\r\n150%;color:#333333;background:white\">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 3. </span><span style=\"font-size:\r\n12.0pt;line-height:150%;color:#333333;background:white\">耳念珠菌已经引发了大规模感染。因此，快速鉴别出耳念珠菌并进行特殊隔离治疗才能有效防止其进一步传播。</span></span></p>\r\n	<p class=\"MsoNormal\">\r\n		<span style=\"font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%;\r\ncolor:#333333;background:white\"><span lang=\"EN-US\" style=\"font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:\r\n10.5pt\">&nbsp;</span></span></p>\r\n	<p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-indent:23.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:2.0;\r\nline-height:150%\">\r\n		<span style=\"font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%;\r\ncolor:#333333;background:white\"><span style=\"font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.5pt;\r\nline-height:150%\">所以，高效、快速和准确的临床检测手段是关键，而联合用药仍是目前主要方案。耳念珠菌的最佳治疗方法尚未确定，棘白菌素是一线治疗药物，可与伏立康唑联合，二者似乎具有协同作用。在治疗无反应的情况下应给予两性霉素<span lang=\"EN-US\">B</span>，如与其他抗真菌剂（例如，棘白菌素）联合应用，则不排除协同效应。然而，由于在治疗期间可能产生耐药性，因此必须予定期药敏试验以确认治疗有效性。较新的唑类（例如泊沙康唑和艾沙康唑）已显示对耳念珠菌具有良好的体外活性。</span></span></p>\r\n	<p class=\"MsoNormal\">\r\n		<span style=\"font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%;\r\ncolor:#333333;background:white\"><span lang=\"EN-US\" style=\"font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:\r\n10.5pt\">&nbsp;</span></span></p>\r\n	<p align=\"left\" class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align:left;line-height:200%\">\r\n		<span style=\"font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%;\r\ncolor:#333333;background:white\"><b style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight:normal\"><span style=\"font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:\r\n10.5pt;line-height:200%;font-family:&quot;微软雅黑&quot;,sans-serif;color:red\">实验室的检测方法：</span></b></span></p>\r\n	<p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-indent:23.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:2.0;\r\nline-height:150%\">\r\n		<span style=\"font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%;\r\ncolor:#333333;background:white\"><span style=\"font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%\">以往的研究表明，血液、尿液、呼吸道和脑脊液等样本中都可以分离出耳念珠菌。但是，由于耳念珠菌在表型上与其他致病的念珠菌难以区分，特别是希木龙假丝酵母菌等，它们同属于希木龙假丝酵母菌复合群<span lang=\"EN-US\">(Candida haemulonii complex)</span>，</span></span></p>\r\n	<p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height:150%\">\r\n		<span style=\"font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%;\r\ncolor:#333333;background:white\"><span style=\"font-size:12.0pt;\r\nline-height:150%\">这是包括了<span lang=\"EN-US\">Candida auris</span>，<span lang=\"EN-US\">Candida duobushaemulonii</span>和<span lang=\"EN-US\">Candida haemulonii</span>在内的一类酵母菌，他们在生化反应表型上十分相似。这使得实验室中常用的显色培养基、生化检测（<span lang=\"EN-US\">API</span>）或者<span lang=\"EN-US\">VITEK2</span>等自动检测仪等，均不能有效准确的检测出该类细菌，亦或错误地判定为其它类型的念珠菌。例如，哥伦比亚卡塔赫纳市<span lang=\"EN-US\">2016</span>年<span lang=\"EN-US\">8</span>月，在儿童重症监护室中检测到<span lang=\"EN-US\">5</span>例耳道念珠菌感染病例，这些分离珠最初被鉴定为白念珠菌和红酵母菌，但最终证实为耳念珠菌；我国已知<span lang=\"EN-US\">18</span>例感染者中，<span lang=\"EN-US\">15</span>例在中国医科大学附属第一医院被发现，初期患者临床标本被分离出<span lang=\"EN-US\">35</span>株希木龙假丝酵母菌，进一步检测后才发现是耳念珠菌。事实上，因常规诊断经常错误识别，耳念珠菌感染的真实流行状况仍然是未知的；所以，高效准确地鉴定耳念珠菌是临床治疗和有效控制该类感染的关键。目前，欧美国家常用的实验室检测方法主要有<span lang=\"EN-US\">:</span></span></span></p>\r\n	<p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height:150%\">\r\n		<span style=\"font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%;\r\ncolor:#333333;background:white\"><span lang=\"EN-US\" style=\"font-size:\r\n12.0pt;line-height:150%\">&nbsp;</span></span></p>\r\n	<p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height:150%\">\r\n		<span style=\"font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%;\r\ncolor:#333333;background:white\"><span style=\"font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%;color:black;background:white\">1. 基于辅助激光解析电离飞行时间质谱仪（</span><span lang=\"EN-US\" style=\"font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif;\r\ncolor:black;background:white\">MALDI-TOF</span><span style=\"font-size:\r\n12.0pt;line-height:150%;color:black;background:white\">）的检测方法。<span lang=\"EN-US\">&nbsp;</span></span></span></p>\r\n	<p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-indent:23.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:2.0;\r\nline-height:150%\">\r\n		<span style=\"font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%;\r\ncolor:#333333;background:white\"><span lang=\"EN-US\" style=\"font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%\">2018</span><span style=\"font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%\">年<span lang=\"EN-US\">4</span>月美国<span lang=\"EN-US\">FDA</span>批准了首个鉴定耳念珠菌方法&mdash;&mdash;</span><span lang=\"EN-US\" style=\"font-size:\r\n12.0pt;line-height:150%;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif\">Bruker MALDI Biotyper CA</span><span style=\"font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%\">系统。</span><span lang=\"EN-US\" style=\"font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif\">Bruker MALDI Biotyper CA</span><span style=\"font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%\">系统采用</span><span lang=\"EN-US\" style=\"font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif\">MALDI-TOF</span><span style=\"font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%\">质谱与微生物数据库相结合的技术。用患者样本培养的菌落，经过</span><span lang=\"EN-US\" style=\"font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif\">MALDI-TOF</span><span style=\"font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%\">质谱仪测定，获得微生物独特的质谱图，与数据库里的谱峰比对，最终得到种水平可靠的鉴定结果。</span></span></p>\r\n	<p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-indent:23.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:2.0;\r\nline-height:150%\">\r\n		<span style=\"font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%;\r\ncolor:#333333;background:white\"><span lang=\"EN-US\" style=\"font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%;\r\nfont-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif\">Bruker MALDI Biotyper CA</span><span style=\"font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%\">系统能够可靠的、大范围地鉴定病原菌，快速鉴定引起院感爆发的病原体，提高实验室常规检测大批样本的能力，改进治疗方案和对病人的有效护理。</span></span></p>\r\n	<p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height:150%\">\r\n		<span style=\"font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%;\r\ncolor:#333333;background:white\"><span lang=\"EN-US\" style=\"font-size:\r\n12.0pt;line-height:150%\">&nbsp;</span></span></p>\r\n	<p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height:150%\">\r\n		<span style=\"font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%;\r\ncolor:#333333;background:white\"><span style=\"font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%;color:black;background:white\">2. 基于基因组测序的方法。</span></span></p>\r\n	<p align=\"left\" class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align:left;text-indent:24.0pt;\r\nmso-char-indent-count:2.0;line-height:150%;mso-pagination:widow-orphan;\r\nbackground:white\">\r\n		<span style=\"font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%;\r\ncolor:#333333;background:white\"><span style=\"font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%;mso-bidi-font-family:\r\n宋体;color:black;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-bidi-font-weight:bold\">目前，已有的真菌基因组序列数据库促进了表型相近和系统进化相似菌类的可靠性鉴定，该方法对于人们确定和研究耳念珠菌的致病性和规律仍然不可或缺。</span></span></p>\r\n	<p align=\"left\" class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align:left;text-indent:24.0pt;\r\nmso-char-indent-count:2.0;line-height:150%;mso-pagination:widow-orphan;\r\nbackground:white\">\r\n		<span style=\"font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%;\r\ncolor:#333333;background:white\"><span style=\"font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%;mso-bidi-font-family:\r\n宋体;color:black;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-bidi-font-weight:bold\">例</span><span style=\"font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;color:#222222;\r\nletter-spacing:0pt;mso-bidi-font-weight:bold\">如对于核糖体<span lang=\"EN-US\">RNA</span>基因（<span lang=\"EN-US\">D1 / D2</span>区域）或内部转录间隔区域（<span lang=\"EN-US\">ITS1</span>和<span lang=\"EN-US\">ITS2</span>区域）的测序，可以提供正确和可靠的耳念珠菌表征；</span><span style=\"font-size:\r\n12.0pt;line-height:150%;mso-bidi-font-family:Arial;color:black;letter-spacing:\r\n0pt;mso-bidi-font-weight:bold\">但测序方法仍然面对着普及、操作繁琐和检测效率低等问题。</span></span></p>\r\n	<br />\r\n	<br />\r\n	<p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-indent: 20pt; line-height: 150%; text-align: center;\">\r\n		&nbsp;</p>\r\n	<p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-indent: 20pt; line-height: 150%;\">\r\n		&nbsp;</p>\r\n	<br />\r\n	<div>\r\n		<span style=\"font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.5pt;font-family:宋体;\r\nmso-bidi-font-family:&quot;Times New widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-size: 16px; line-height: 20.48px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);\">\r\n		&ldquo;TORCH&rdquo;一词最早由AndreNahmias在上世纪70年代提出，指的是一组在孕期感染可能会导致胎儿畸形和功能障碍的病原微生物。&ldquo;T&rdquo;指的是弓形虫（Toxoplasmosis），&ldquo;O&rdquo;指的是其他病原微生物（Others），&ldquo;R&rdquo;指的是风疹病毒（Rubella），&ldquo;C&rdquo;指的是巨细胞病毒（Cytomegalovirus），&ldquo;H&rdquo;指的是单纯疱疹病毒（Herpes simplex virus）。</p>\r\n	<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; overflow-wrap: break-word !important; clear: both; min-height: 1em; font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: 0.544px; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-size: 16px; line-height: 20.48px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255); text-align: center;\">\r\n		<img alt=\"\" src=\"/uploads/allimg/190816/1-1ZQ615015a93.jpg\" style=\"width: 424px; height: 377px;\" /></p>\r\n	<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; overflow-wrap: break-word !important; clear: both; min-height: 1em; font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: 0.544px; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-size: 16px; line-height: 20.48px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);\">\r\n		&nbsp;</p>\r\n	<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; clear: both; min-height: 1em; font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: 0.544px; orphans: 2; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-size: 16px; line-height: 20.48px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);\">\r\n		TORCH感染主要特点是孕妇感染后无症状或症状轻微，但有可能垂直传播给胎儿，引起宫内感染，导致流产、死胎、早产和先天畸形等，即使幸存，也可能遗留中枢神经系统等损害。</p>\r\n	<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; clear: both; min-height: 1em; font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: 0.544px; orphans: 2; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-size: 16px; line-height: 20.48px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);\">\r\n		&nbsp;</p>\r\n	<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; clear: both; min-height: 1em; font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: 0.544px; orphans: 2; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-size: 16px; line-height: 20.48px; text-align: center; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);\">\r\n		<strong style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">我们需要知道以下两点：</strong></p>\r\n	<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; clear: both; min-height: 1em; font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: 0.544px; orphans: 2; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-size: 16px; line-height: 20.48px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);\">\r\n		1.孕妇TORCH感染, 胎儿不一定被感染。</p>\r\n	<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; clear: both; min-height: 1em; font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: 0.544px; orphans: 2; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-size: 16px; line-height: 20.48px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);\">\r\n		2.胎儿宫内感染不一定会导致胎儿先天缺陷。</p>\r\n	<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; clear: both; min-height: 1em; font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: 0.544px; orphans: 2; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-size: 16px; line-height: 20.48px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);\">\r\n		&nbsp;</p>\r\n	<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; clear: both; min-height: 1em; font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: 0.544px; orphans: 2; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-size: 16px; line-height: 20.48px; text-align: center; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);\">\r\n		<strong style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">TORCH检查的目的是什么？</strong></p>\r\n	<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; clear: both; min-height: 1em; font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: 0.544px; orphans: 2; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-size: 16px; line-height: 20.48px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);\">\r\n		1.孕前检查：可评估育龄妇女的免疫力，了解其是否已感染过相关病原体。若没有感染过则属于怀孕后容易出问题的高危人群，可考虑注射疫苗、加强孕期监测等措施。</p>\r\n	<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; clear: both; min-height: 1em; font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: 0.544px; orphans: 2; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-size: 16px; line-height: 20.48px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);\">\r\n		2.孕期检查：可以与孕前情况作比对，判断孕妇感染的状态，评估产前诊断宫内感染的必要性。</p>\r\n	<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; clear: both; min-height: 1em; font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: 0.544px; orphans: 2; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-size: 16px; line-height: 20.48px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);\">\r\n		3.出生后检查：对新生儿进行TORCH检查，可提供产后先天感染的证据。</p>\r\n	<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; clear: both; min-height: 1em; font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: 0.544px; orphans: 2; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-size: 16px; line-height: 20.48px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);\">\r\n		&nbsp;</p>\r\n	<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; clear: both; min-height: 1em; font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: 0.544px; orphans: 2; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-size: 16px; line-height: 20.48px; text-align: center; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);\">\r\n		<strong style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">TORCH检测的指标有哪些？</strong></p>\r\n	<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; clear: both; min-height: 1em; font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: 0.544px; orphans: 2; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-size: 16px; line-height: 20.48px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);\">\r\n		（一）间接指标：主要是IgG和IgM抗体，这是病原体感染后人体产生的免疫反应指标，与个体的免疫功能有关，主要用于感染的筛查和免疫状态的评估。</p>\r\n	<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; clear: both; min-height: 1em; font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: 0.544px; orphans: 2; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-size: 16px; line-height: 20.48px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);\">\r\n		IgM抗体：如果是IgM抗体（＋），一般情况下说明是近期感染，但是在某些情况下，IgM抗体会持续长久存在，所以IgM抗体（＋）并不能简单地等同于近期感染。</p>\r\n	<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; clear: both; min-height: 1em; font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: 0.544px; orphans: 2; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-size: 16px; line-height: 20.48px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);\">\r\n		IgG抗体：说明既往感染，有一定的免疫水平。当患者发生复发感染时， IgM 和 IgG 都能较快地上升到较高滴度，其中 IgG 上升极其显著（一般可上升4倍以上的水平）。</p>\r\n	<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; clear: both; min-height: 1em; font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: 0.544px; orphans: 2; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-size: 16px; line-height: 20.48px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);\">\r\n		IgG 亲和力：IgG 亲和力可以帮助我们确认病原体感染时间，一般情况下IgG 亲和力高说明是远期感染，亲和力低说明是近期感染。</p>\r\n	<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; clear: both; min-height: 1em; font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: 0.544px; orphans: 2; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-size: 16px; line-height: 20.48px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);\">\r\n		抗体定量检查：简单的抗体定性检查无法很好帮助我们判断究竟是近期感染还是远期感染，可以进行不同时间段的抗体定量检查，根据抗体滴度水平的变化来帮助判断。</p>\r\n	<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; clear: both; min-height: 1em; font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: 0.544px; orphans: 2; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-size: 16px; line-height: 20.48px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);\">\r\n		（二）直接指标：主要是利用分子诊断的方法（例如PCR）来对病原体本身进行检查，用于TORCH感染的诊断。</p>\r\n	<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; clear: both; min-height: 1em; font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: 0.544px; orphans: 2; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-size: 16px; line-height: 20.48px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);\">\r\n		&nbsp;</p>\r\n	<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; clear: both; min-height: 1em; font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: 0.544px; orphans: 2; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-size: 16px; line-height: 20.48px; text-align: center; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);\">\r\n		<strong style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">&ldquo;TORCH&rdquo;感染意味着什么？该怎么办？</strong></p>\r\n	<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; clear: both; min-height: 1em; font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: 0.544px; orphans: 2; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-size: 16px; line-height: 20.48px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);\">\r\n		<strong style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">【弓形虫】</strong></p>\r\n	<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; overflow-wrap: break-word !important; clear: both; min-height: 1em; font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: 0.544px; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-size: 16px; line-height: 20.48px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255); text-align: center;\">\r\n		<strong style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><img alt=\"\" src=\"/uploads/allimg/190816/1-1ZQ6150254b2.jpg\" style=\"width: 345px; height: 221px;\" /></strong></p>\r\n	<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; overflow-wrap: break-word !important; clear: both; min-height: 1em; font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: 0.544px; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-size: 16px; line-height: 20.48px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);\">\r\n		&nbsp;</p>\r\n	<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; clear: both; min-height: 1em; font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: 0.544px; orphans: 2; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-size: 16px; line-height: 20.48px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);\">\r\n		弓形虫是一种人畜共患疾病，猫与其他动物是传染源。孕妇弓形虫感染通常是摄取了弓形虫卵囊污染的食物和水引起。孕妇感染后几乎没有临床状，少数可有淋巴结肿大的表现。其主要危害在于若妊娠期初次感染弓形虫，有可引起胎儿宫内感染从而导致胎儿视觉和听觉丧失、智力和精神运动发育迟滞、癫痫发作、血液系统异常、肝脾肿大、甚至死亡。</p>\r\n	<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; clear: both; min-height: 1em; font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: 0.544px; orphans: 2; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-size: 16px; line-height: 20.48px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);\">\r\n		【建议】由于弓形虫传染源是动物，感染途径主要是与动物密切接触和生食肉类。建议注意手卫生，不要吃半生不熟的肉类，生熟炊具分开使用。高危人群孕前筛查，被确诊为初次感染者建议6个月后再怀孕。</p>\r\n	<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; clear: both; min-height: 1em; font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: 0.544px; orphans: 2; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-size: 16px; line-height: 20.48px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);\">\r\n		&nbsp;</p>\r\n	<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; clear: both; min-height: 1em; font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: 0.544px; orphans: 2; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-size: 16px; line-height: 20.48px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);\">\r\n		<strong style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">【风疹病毒】</strong></p>\r\n	<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; clear: both; min-height: 1em; font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: 0.544px; orphans: 2; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-size: 16px; line-height: 20.48px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);\">\r\n		风疹病毒（RV）是一种单链RNA病毒，经鼻咽飞沫传播。孕妇感染后大部分无明显症状或症状轻微，部分孕妇可表现为不典型的感冒症状或颜面部、躯干和四肢出现特征性红色斑丘疹。</p>\r\n	<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; overflow-wrap: break-word !important; clear: both; min-height: 1em; font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: 0.544px; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-size: 16px; line-height: 20.48px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255); text-align: center;\">\r\n		&nbsp;</p>\r\n</div>\r\n<div style=\"text-align: center;\">\r\n	<span style=\"color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: 0.544px; orphans: 2; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255); display: inline !important; float: none;\"><img alt=\"\" src=\"/uploads/allimg/190816/1-1ZQ6150341405.jpg\" style=\"width: 357px; height: 225px;\" /></span></div>\r\n<div>\r\n	<br />\r\n	<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; clear: both; min-height: 1em; font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: 0.544px; orphans: 2; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-size: 16px; line-height: 20.48px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);\">\r\n		其主要危害在于若妊娠期初次感染风疹病毒，将有很高的宫内感染率并可能导致胎儿先天风疹综合征，主要表现为眼、心血管系统和中枢神经系统发育异常。在孕11周前发生的风疹宫内感染所导致的胎儿出生缺陷率高达90%，以后逐渐下降，在孕16周以后感染风疹一般不会导致先天畸形，但可导致胎儿生长受限（FGR）。</p>\r\n	<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; clear: both; min-height: 1em; font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: 0.544px; orphans: 2; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-size: 16px; line-height: 20.48px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);\">\r\n		【建议】由于国内接近10%~15%的妇女RV-IgG阴性，在RV流行的时候容易受到感染，因此需要进行主动免疫。建议准备生育的妇女在孕前常规进行RV-IgM、IgG抗体定量测定，RV-IgG抗体阴性的妇女应到当地疾病防御控制中心注射麻风腮三联疫苗，避孕1~3个月后再计划妊娠。</p>\r\n	<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; clear: both; min-height: 1em; font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: 0.544px; orphans: 2; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-size: 16px; line-height: 20.48px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);\">\r\n		&nbsp;</p>\r\n	<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; clear: both; min-height: 1em; font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: 0.544px; orphans: 2; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-size: 16px; line-height: 20.48px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);\">\r\n		<strong style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">【巨细胞病毒】</strong></p>\r\n	<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; clear: both; min-height: 1em; font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: 0.544px; orphans: 2; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-size: 16px; line-height: 20.48px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);\">\r\n		孕妇感染巨细胞病毒造成的危害远大于弓形虫、风疹和单纯疱疹病毒，这一观点在全球范围内的研究结论都是一致的，已达成共识。</p>\r\n	<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; overflow-wrap: break-word !important; clear: both; min-height: 1em; font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: 0.544px; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-size: 16px; line-height: 20.48px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);\">\r\n		巨细胞病毒（CMV）为DNA病毒, 可通过唾液、尿液、宫颈分泌物、精液、血液等传播。孕妇感染后通常没有症状或仅表现为一般的不适、发热、咽炎、淋巴结肿大等。</p>\r\n	<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; overflow-wrap: break-word !important; clear: both; min-height: 1em; font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: 0.544px; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-size: 16px; line-height: 20.48px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255); text-align: center;\">\r\n		<img alt=\"\" src=\"/uploads/allimg/190816/1-1ZQ615041O53.jpg\" style=\"width: 348px; height: 222px;\" /></p>\r\n	<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; overflow-wrap: break-word !important; clear: both; min-height: 1em; font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: 0.544px; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-size: 16px; line-height: 20.48px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);\">\r\n		&nbsp;</p>\r\n</div>\r\n<br />\r\n<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; clear: both; min-height: 1em; font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: 0.544px; orphans: 2; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-size: 16px; line-height: 20.48px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);\">\r\n	其主要危害在于若妊娠期发生宫内感染，可能引起胎儿生长受限、小头畸形, 肝脾肿大、黄疸、脉络膜视网膜炎、血小板减少以及贫血等发育异常，并可能导致婴儿感音神经性耳聋、精神运动发育迟缓和视觉障碍等远期并发症。</p>\r\n<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; clear: both; min-height: 1em; font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: 0.544px; orphans: 2; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-size: 16px; line-height: 20.48px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);\">\r\n	&nbsp;</p>\r\n<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; clear: both; min-height: 1em; font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: 0.544px; orphans: 2; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-size: 16px; line-height: 20.48px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);\">\r\n	【建议】孕期CMV原发性感染率0.7%~4%，但其导致的胎儿垂直感染率高达30%~40%。孕期CMV复发感染导致垂直感染率仅为0.15%~2%，但因CMV复发感染孕妇基数大，导致复发感染人数要远多于原发性感染造成的新生儿CMV感染。因此，需要重视对CMV复发感染和再次感染的监测，在早、中、晚孕期定量测定尿液CMV-DNA或定期检测CMV-IgM、IgG变化，评估产前诊断的必要性。&nbsp;</p>\r\n<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; clear: both; min-height: 1em; font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: 0.544px; orphans: 2; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-size: 16px; line-height: 20.48px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);\">\r\n	&nbsp;</p>\r\n<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; clear: both; min-height: 1em; font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: 0.544px; orphans: 2; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-size: 16px; line-height: 20.48px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);\">\r\n	【单纯疱疹病毒】</p>\r\n<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; clear: both; min-height: 1em; font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: 0.544px; orphans: 2; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-size: 16px; line-height: 20.48px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);\">\r\n	单纯疱疹病毒（HSV）为DNA病毒, 可分成HSV-Ⅰ和HSV-Ⅱ两种血清型。HSV-Ⅰ主要通过直接、间接接触或飞沫传播，感染口腔、皮肤、黏膜、眼黏膜及中枢神经系统，偶见于外生殖器；HSV-Ⅱ通常为性传播，引起生殖系统感染，偶见于口腔病变。HSV一经感染终身携带，病毒潜伏在神经节。</p>\r\n<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; overflow-wrap: break-word !important; clear: both; min-height: 1em; font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: 0.544px; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-size: 16px; line-height: 20.48px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255); text-align: center;\">\r\n	<img alt=\"\" src=\"/uploads/allimg/190816/1-1ZQ6150514608.jpg\" style=\"width: 164px; height: 221px;\" /></p>\r\n<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; overflow-wrap: break-word !important; clear: both; min-height: 1em; font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: 0.544px; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-size: 16px; line-height: 20.48px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);\">\r\n	&nbsp;</p>\r\n<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; clear: both; min-height: 1em; font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: 0.544px; orphans: 2; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-size: 16px; line-height: 20.48px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);\">\r\n	【建议】我国成人多数已有过单纯疱疹病毒感染，多数妇女也已经获得抗单纯疱疹病毒的特异性抗体，这类病毒引起的宫内感染很罕见。HSV感染胎儿的主要途径是通过产道感染新生儿，经胎盘垂直传播罕见。孕早、中期即使孕妇发生初次感染，造成胎儿感染的概率也极低，孕早期筛查意义不大。</p>\r\n<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; clear: both; min-height: 1em; font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: 0.544px; orphans: 2; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-size: 16px; line-height: 20.48px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);\">\r\n	由于HSV-Ⅰ和HSV-Ⅱ这两种病毒型对胎儿危害和临床治疗方法没有区别，所以，围孕期进行HSV血清学筛查时没必要分型检测。</p>\r\n<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; clear: both; min-height: 1em; font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: 0.544px; orphans: 2; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-size: 16px; line-height: 20.48px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);\">\r\n	HSV血清学筛查常常遇到IgM抗体假阳性和IgM抗体长期携带的困扰。若无临床症状不需要等待其IgM抗体转阴再妊娠。</p>\r\n<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; clear: both; min-height: 1em; font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: 0.544px; orphans: 2; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-size: 16px; line-height: 20.48px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);\">\r\n	由于有生殖道HSV感染的产妇经阴道分娩时垂直传播给新生儿的风险是30%~50%，在孕晚期可进行阴道分泌物HSV定量PCR检测，根据检测结果和临床症状给予治疗和确定分娩方式。&nbsp;</p>\r\n<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; clear: both; min-height: 1em; font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: 0.544px; orphans: 2; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-size: 16px; line-height: 20.48px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);\">\r\n	&nbsp;</p>\r\n<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; clear: both; min-height: 1em; font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: 0.544px; orphans: 2; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-size: 16px; line-height: 20.48px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);\">\r\n	说了这么多，孕妈妈们拿到TORCH报告看到有&ldquo;阳性&rdquo;结果再不要盲目的陷入焦虑和恐慌中啦~</p>\r\n<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; overflow-wrap: break-word !important; clear: both; min-height: 1em; font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: 0.544px; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-size: 16px; line-height: 20.48px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255); text-align: center;\">\r\n	<img alt=\"\" src=\"/uploads/allimg/190816/1-1ZQ6150602Q0.jpg\" style=\"width: 327px; height: 198px;\" /></p>\r\n<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; clear: both; min-height: 1em; font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: 0.544px; orphans: 2; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-size: 16px; line-height: 20.48px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);\">\r\n	目前，TORCH 筛查并不是孕前或孕期检查的必查项目。但是，根据 2011 年中华医学会妇产科学会产科学组发布的《孕前和孕期保健指南》：TORCH筛查被列为孕前3个月首选备查项目。如果怀孕后发现急性感染，可能发生的流产、早产、宫内死胎等，会给准妈妈和家人造成巨大的心理负担，这是谁都不愿意看到的情况。所以，孕前TORCH检查非常重要，每一位打算怀孕的女性都应该在准备怀孕前至少提前三个月做此检查，检查报告应由专业医生解释评估。高风险人群更是不应该错过此项孕前检查。希望各位备孕女性及孕妈妈们都能重视产前筛查与产前诊断，避免宝宝的出生缺陷。</p>\r\n<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; clear: both; min-height: 1em; font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: 0.544px; orphans: 2; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-size: 16px; line-height: 20.48px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);\">\r\n	&nbsp;</p>\r\n<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; clear: both; min-height: 1em; font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: 0.544px; orphans: 2; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-size: 16px; line-height: 20.48px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);\">\r\n	来源：华西第二医院产前诊断中心</p>\r\n<br class=\"Apple-interchange-newline\" />\r\n<p style=\"margin: 0px;
